646:// src/logger/log-warnings.ts
647:function formatWarning({
648:  warning,
649:  provider,
650:  model
651:}) {
652:  const prefix = `AI SDK Warning (${provider} / ${model}):`;
653:  switch (warning.type) {
654:    case "unsupported": {
655:      let message = `${prefix} The feature "${warning.feature}" is not supported.`;
656:      if (warning.details) {
657:        message += ` ${warning.details}`;
658:      }
659:      return message;
660:    }
661:    case "compatibility": {
662:      let message = `${prefix} The feature "${warning.feature}" is used in a compatibility mode.`;
663:      if (warning.details) {
664:        message += ` ${warning.details}`;
665:      }
666:      return message;
667:    }
668:    case "other": {
669:      return `${prefix} ${warning.message}`;
670:    }
671:    default: {
672:      return `${prefix} ${JSON.stringify(warning, null, 2)}`;
673:    }
674:  }
675:}
676:var FIRST_WARNING_INFO_MESSAGE = "AI SDK Warning System: To turn off warning logging, set the AI_SDK_LOG_WARNINGS global to false.";
677:var hasLoggedBefore = false;
678:var logWarnings = (options) => {
679:  if (options.warnings.length === 0) {
680:    return;
681:  }
682:  const logger = globalThis.AI_SDK_LOG_WARNINGS;
683:  if (logger === false) {
684:    return;
685:  }
686:  if (typeof logger === "function") {
687:    logger(options);
688:    return;
689:  }
690:  if (!hasLoggedBefore) {
691:    hasLoggedBefore = true;
692:    console.info(FIRST_WARNING_INFO_MESSAGE);
693:  }
694:  for (const warning of options.warnings) {
695:    console.warn(
696:      formatWarning({
697:        warning,
698:        provider: options.provider,
699:        model: options.model
700:      })
701:    );
702:  }

762:// src/model/as-language-model-v3.ts
763:function asLanguageModelV3(model) {
764:  if (model.specificationVersion === "v3") {
765:    return model;
766:  }
767:  logV2CompatibilityWarning({
768:    provider: model.provider,
769:    modelId: model.modelId
770:  });
771:  return new Proxy(model, {
772:    get(target, prop) {
773:      switch (prop) {
774:        case "specificationVersion":
775:          return "v3";
776:        case "doGenerate":
777:          return async (...args) => {
778:            const result = await target.doGenerate(...args);
779:            return {
780:              ...result,
781:              finishReason: convertV2FinishReasonToV3(result.finishReason),
782:              usage: convertV2UsageToV3(result.usage)
783:            };
784:          };
785:        case "doStream":
786:          return async (...args) => {
787:            const result = await target.doStream(...args);
788:            return {
789:              ...result,
790:              stream: convertV2StreamToV3(result.stream)
791:            };
792:          };
793:        default:
794:          return target[prop];
795:      }
796:    }
797:  });
798:}
799:function convertV2StreamToV3(stream) {
800:  return stream.pipeThrough(
801:    new TransformStream({
802:      transform(chunk, controller) {
803:        switch (chunk.type) {
804:          case "finish":
805:            controller.enqueue({
806:              ...chunk,
807:              finishReason: convertV2FinishReasonToV3(chunk.finishReason),
808:              usage: convertV2UsageToV3(chunk.usage)
809:            });
810:            break;
811:          default:
812:            controller.enqueue(chunk);
813:            break;
814:        }
815:      }
816:    })
817:  );
818:}
819:function convertV2FinishReasonToV3(finishReason) {
820:  return {
821:    unified: finishReason === "unknown" ? "other" : finishReason,
822:    raw: void 0
823:  };
824:}

826:  return {
827:    inputTokens: {
828:      total: usage.inputTokens,
829:      noCache: void 0,
830:      cacheRead: usage.cachedInputTokens,
831:      cacheWrite: void 0
832:    },
833:    outputTokens: {
834:      total: usage.outputTokens,
835:      text: void 0,
836:      reasoning: usage.reasoningTokens
837:    }
838:  };
839:}

1222:  const bytes = typeof data === "string" ? (0, import_provider_utils2.convertBase64ToUint8Array)(data) : data;
1223:  const id3Size = (bytes[6] & 127) << 21 | (bytes[7] & 127) << 14 | (bytes[8] & 127) << 7 | bytes[9] & 127;
1224:  return bytes.slice(id3Size + 10);
1225:};
1226:function stripID3TagsIfPresent(data) {

1228:  data[1] === 68 && // 'D'
1229:  data[2] === 51;

1232:function detectMediaType({
1233:  data,
1234:  signatures
1235:}) {
1236:  const processedData = stripID3TagsIfPresent(data);

1238:    processedData.substring(0, Math.min(processedData.length, 24))
1239:  ) : processedData;

1241:    if (bytes.length >= signature.bytesPrefix.length && signature.bytesPrefix.every(
1242:      (byte, index) => byte === null || bytes[index] === byte
1243:    )) {
1244:      return signature.mediaType;
1245:    }
1246:  }
1247:  return void 0;

1507:function convertToLanguageModelMessage({

1638:async function downloadAssets(messages, download2, supportedUrls) {

1674:function convertPartToLanguageModelPart(part, downloadedAssets) {
1675:  var _a21;
1676:  if (part.type === "text") {
1677:    return {
1678:      type: "text",
1679:      text: part.text,
1680:      providerOptions: part.providerOptions
1681:    };
1682:  }
1683:  let originalData;
1684:  const type = part.type;
1685:  switch (type) {
1686:    case "image":
1687:      originalData = part.image;
1688:      break;
1689:    case "file":
1690:      originalData = part.data;
1691:      break;
1692:    default:
1693:      throw new Error(`Unsupported part type: ${type}`);
1694:  }
1695:  const { data: convertedData, mediaType: convertedMediaType } = convertToLanguageModelV3DataContent(originalData);
1696:  let mediaType = convertedMediaType != null ? convertedMediaType : part.mediaType;
1697:  let data = convertedData;
1698:  if (data instanceof URL) {
1699:    const downloadedFile = downloadedAssets[data.toString()];
1700:    if (downloadedFile) {
1701:      data = downloadedFile.data;
1702:      mediaType != null ? mediaType : mediaType = downloadedFile.mediaType;
1703:    }
1704:  }
1705:  switch (type) {
1706:    case "image": {
1707:      if (data instanceof Uint8Array || typeof data === "string") {

1709:      }

1711:        type: "file",
1712:        mediaType: mediaType != null ? mediaType : "image/*",
1713:        // any image
1714:        filename: void 0,
1715:        data,
1716:        providerOptions: part.providerOptions
1717:      };
1718:    }
1719:    case "file": {
1720:      if (mediaType == null) {
1721:        throw new Error(`Media type is missing for file part`);
1722:      }
1723:      return {
1724:        type: "file",
1725:        mediaType,
1726:        filename: part.filename,
1727:        data,
1728:        providerOptions: part.providerOptions
1729:      };
1730:    }
1731:  }

1733:function mapToolResultOutput(output) {

1735:    return output;
1736:  }
1737:  return {

1740:      if (item.type !== "media") {

1744:        return {
1745:          type: "image-data",
1746:          data: item.data,
1747:          mediaType: item.mediaType

1750:      return {
1751:        type: "file-data",
1752:        data: item.data,
1753:        mediaType: item.mediaType

2146:// src/prompt/standardize-prompt.ts
2147:async function standardizePrompt(prompt) {
2148:  if (prompt.prompt == null && prompt.messages == null) {
2149:    throw new import_provider24.InvalidPromptError({
2150:      prompt,
2151:      message: "prompt or messages must be defined"
2152:    });
2153:  }
2154:  if (prompt.prompt != null && prompt.messages != null) {
2155:    throw new import_provider24.InvalidPromptError({
2156:      prompt,
2157:      message: "prompt and messages cannot be defined at the same time"
2158:    });
2159:  }
2160:  if (prompt.system != null && typeof prompt.system !== "string" && !asArray(prompt.system).every(
2161:    (message) => typeof message === "object" && message !== null && "role" in message && message.role === "system"
2162:  )) {
2163:    throw new import_provider24.InvalidPromptError({
2164:      prompt,
2165:      message: "system must be a string, SystemModelMessage, or array of SystemModelMessage"
2166:    });
2167:  }
2168:  let messages;
2169:  if (prompt.prompt != null && typeof prompt.prompt === "string") {
2170:    messages = [{ role: "user", content: prompt.prompt }];
2171:  } else if (prompt.prompt != null && Array.isArray(prompt.prompt)) {
2172:    messages = prompt.prompt;
2173:  } else if (prompt.messages != null) {
2174:    messages = prompt.messages;
2175:  } else {
2176:    throw new import_provider24.InvalidPromptError({
2177:      prompt,
2178:      message: "prompt or messages must be defined"
2179:    });
2180:  }
2181:  if (messages.length === 0) {
2182:    throw new import_provider24.InvalidPromptError({
2183:      prompt,
2184:      message: "messages must not be empty"
2185:    });
2186:  }
2187:  const validationResult = await (0, import_provider_utils8.safeValidateTypes)({
2188:    value: messages,
2189:    schema: import_v46.z.array(modelMessageSchema)
2190:  });
2191:  if (!validationResult.success) {
2192:    throw new import_provider24.InvalidPromptError({
2193:      prompt,
2194:      message: "The messages do not match the ModelMessage[] schema.",
2195:      cause: validationResult.error
2196:    });
2197:  }
2198:  return {
2199:    messages,
2200:    system: prompt.system
2201:  };
2202:}

2366:var import_api2 = require("@opentelemetry/api");
2367:async function recordSpan({
2368:  name: name21,
2369:  tracer,
2370:  attributes,
2371:  fn,
2372:  endWhenDone = true
2373:}) {
2374:  return tracer.startActiveSpan(
2375:    name21,
2376:    { attributes: await attributes },
2377:    async (span) => {
2378:      const ctx = import_api2.context.active();
2379:      try {
2380:        const result = await import_api2.context.with(ctx, () => fn(span));
2381:        if (endWhenDone) {
2382:          span.end();
2383:        }
2384:        return result;
2385:      } catch (error) {
2386:        try {
2387:          recordErrorOnSpan(span, error);
2388:        } finally {
2389:          span.end();
2390:        }
2391:        throw error;
2392:      }
2393:    }
2394:  );
2395:}

2398:    span.recordException({
2399:      name: error.name,
2400:      message: error.message,
2401:      stack: error.stack
2402:    });
2403:    span.setStatus({
2404:      code: import_api2.SpanStatusCode.ERROR,
2405:      message: error.message
2406:    });
2407:  } else {
2408:    span.setStatus({ code: import_api2.SpanStatusCode.ERROR });
2409:  }

2616:function mergeObjects(base, overrides) {
2617:  if (base === void 0 && overrides === void 0) {
2618:    return void 0;
2619:  }
2620:  if (base === void 0) {
2621:    return overrides;
2622:  }
2623:  if (overrides === void 0) {
2624:    return base;
2625:  }
2626:  const result = { ...base };
2627:  for (const key in overrides) {
2628:    if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(overrides, key)) {
2629:      const overridesValue = overrides[key];
2630:      if (overridesValue === void 0)
2631:        continue;

2633:      const isSourceObject = overridesValue !== null && typeof overridesValue === "object" && !Array.isArray(overridesValue) && !(overridesValue instanceof Date) && !(overridesValue instanceof RegExp);

2635:      if (isSourceObject && isTargetObject) {
2636:        result[key] = mergeObjects(
2637:          baseValue,
2638:          overridesValue
2639:        );
2640:      } else {

2642:      }
2643:    }

2651:function getRetryDelayInMs({
2652:  error,
2653:  exponentialBackoffDelay
2654:}) {
2655:  const headers = error.responseHeaders;
2656:  if (!headers)
2657:    return exponentialBackoffDelay;
2658:  let ms;
2659:  const retryAfterMs = headers["retry-after-ms"];
2660:  if (retryAfterMs) {
2661:    const timeoutMs = parseFloat(retryAfterMs);
2662:    if (!Number.isNaN(timeoutMs)) {
2663:      ms = timeoutMs;
2664:    }
2665:  }
2666:  const retryAfter = headers["retry-after"];
2667:  if (retryAfter && ms === void 0) {
2668:    const timeoutSeconds = parseFloat(retryAfter);
2669:    if (!Number.isNaN(timeoutSeconds)) {
2670:      ms = timeoutSeconds * 1e3;
2671:    } else {
2672:      ms = Date.parse(retryAfter) - Date.now();
2673:    }
2674:  }
2675:  if (ms != null && !Number.isNaN(ms) && 0 <= ms && (ms < 60 * 1e3 || ms < exponentialBackoffDelay)) {
2676:    return ms;
2677:  }
2678:  return exponentialBackoffDelay;
2679:}

2683:  backoffFactor = 2,

2691:async function _retryWithExponentialBackoff(f, {
2692:  maxRetries,
2693:  delayInMs,
2694:  backoffFactor,
2695:  abortSignal
2696:}, errors = []) {
2697:  try {
2698:    return await f();
2699:  } catch (error) {
2700:    if ((0, import_provider_utils9.isAbortError)(error)) {
2701:      throw error;
2702:    }
2703:    if (maxRetries === 0) {
2704:      throw error;
2705:    }
2706:    const errorMessage = (0, import_provider_utils9.getErrorMessage)(error);
2707:    const newErrors = [...errors, error];
2708:    const tryNumber = newErrors.length;
2709:    if (tryNumber > maxRetries) {
2710:      throw new RetryError({
2711:        message: `Failed after ${tryNumber} attempts. Last error: ${errorMessage}`,
2712:        reason: "maxRetriesExceeded",
2713:        errors: newErrors
2714:      });
2715:    }
2716:    if (error instanceof Error && import_provider26.APICallError.isInstance(error) && error.isRetryable === true && tryNumber <= maxRetries) {
2717:      await (0, import_provider_utils9.delay)(

2720:          exponentialBackoffDelay: delayInMs
2721:        }),

2723:      );
2724:      return _retryWithExponentialBackoff(
2725:        f,
2726:        {
2727:          maxRetries,
2728:          delayInMs: backoffFactor * delayInMs,
2729:          backoffFactor,
2730:          abortSignal
2731:        },
2732:        newErrors
2733:      );
2734:    }
2735:    if (tryNumber === 1) {
2736:      throw error;
2737:    }
2738:    throw new RetryError({
2739:      message: `Failed after ${tryNumber} attempts with non-retryable error: '${errorMessage}'`,
2740:      reason: "errorNotRetryable",
2741:      errors: newErrors
2742:    });
2743:  }

3235:          case '"': {
3236:            stack.pop();
3237:            lastValidIndex = i;
3238:            break;
3239:          }
3240:          case "\\": {
3241:            stack.push("INSIDE_STRING_ESCAPE");
3242:            break;
3243:          }
3244:          default: {
3245:            lastValidIndex = i;
3246:          }
3247:        }
3248:        break;
3249:      }
3250:      case "INSIDE_ARRAY_START": {
3251:        switch (char) {
3252:          case "]": {
3253:            lastValidIndex = i;
3254:            stack.pop();
3255:            break;
3256:          }
3257:          default: {
3258:            lastValidIndex = i;
3259:            processValueStart(char, i, "INSIDE_ARRAY_AFTER_VALUE");
3260:            break;
3261:          }
3262:        }
3263:        break;
3264:      }
3265:      case "INSIDE_ARRAY_AFTER_VALUE": {
3266:        switch (char) {
3267:          case ",": {
3268:            stack.pop();
3269:            stack.push("INSIDE_ARRAY_AFTER_COMMA");
3270:            break;
3271:          }
3272:          case "]": {
3273:            lastValidIndex = i;
3274:            stack.pop();
3275:            break;
3276:          }
3277:          default: {
3278:            lastValidIndex = i;
3279:            break;
3280:          }
3281:        }
3282:        break;
3283:      }
3284:      case "INSIDE_ARRAY_AFTER_COMMA": {
3285:        processValueStart(char, i, "INSIDE_ARRAY_AFTER_VALUE");
3286:        break;
3287:      }
3288:      case "INSIDE_STRING_ESCAPE": {
3289:        stack.pop();
3290:        lastValidIndex = i;
3291:        break;
3292:      }
3293:      case "INSIDE_NUMBER": {
3294:        switch (char) {
3295:          case "0":
3296:          case "1":
3297:          case "2":
3298:          case "3":
3299:          case "4":
3300:          case "5":
3301:          case "6":
3302:          case "7":
3303:          case "8":
3304:          case "9": {
3305:            lastValidIndex = i;
3306:            break;
3307:          }
3308:          case "e":
3309:          case "E":
3310:          case "-":
3311:          case ".": {
3312:            break;
3313:          }
3314:          case ",": {
3315:            stack.pop();
3316:            if (stack[stack.length - 1] === "INSIDE_ARRAY_AFTER_VALUE") {
3317:              processAfterArrayValue(char, i);
3318:            }
3319:            if (stack[stack.length - 1] === "INSIDE_OBJECT_AFTER_VALUE") {
3320:              processAfterObjectValue(char, i);
3321:            }
3322:            break;
3323:          }
3324:          case "}": {
3325:            stack.pop();
3326:            if (stack[stack.length - 1] === "INSIDE_OBJECT_AFTER_VALUE") {
3327:              processAfterObjectValue(char, i);
3328:            }
3329:            break;
3330:          }
3331:          case "]": {
3332:            stack.pop();
3333:            if (stack[stack.length - 1] === "INSIDE_ARRAY_AFTER_VALUE") {
3334:              processAfterArrayValue(char, i);
3335:            }
3336:            break;
3337:          }
3338:          default: {
3339:            stack.pop();
3340:            break;
3341:          }
3342:        }
3343:        break;
3344:      }
3345:      case "INSIDE_LITERAL": {
3346:        const partialLiteral = input.substring(literalStart, i + 1);
3347:        if (!"false".startsWith(partialLiteral) && !"true".startsWith(partialLiteral) && !"null".startsWith(partialLiteral)) {
3348:          stack.pop();
3349:          if (stack[stack.length - 1] === "INSIDE_OBJECT_AFTER_VALUE") {
3350:            processAfterObjectValue(char, i);
3351:          } else if (stack[stack.length - 1] === "INSIDE_ARRAY_AFTER_VALUE") {
3352:            processAfterArrayValue(char, i);
3353:          }
3354:        } else {
3355:          lastValidIndex = i;
3356:        }
3357:        break;
3358:      }
3359:    }
3360:  }
3361:  let result = input.slice(0, lastValidIndex + 1);
3362:  for (let i = stack.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
3363:    const state = stack[i];
3364:    switch (state) {
3365:      case "INSIDE_STRING": {
3366:        result += '"';
3367:        break;
3368:      }
3369:      case "INSIDE_OBJECT_KEY":
3370:      case "INSIDE_OBJECT_AFTER_KEY":
3371:      case "INSIDE_OBJECT_AFTER_COMMA":
3372:      case "INSIDE_OBJECT_START":
3373:      case "INSIDE_OBJECT_BEFORE_VALUE":
3374:      case "INSIDE_OBJECT_AFTER_VALUE": {
3375:        result += "}";
3376:        break;
3377:      }
3378:      case "INSIDE_ARRAY_START":
3379:      case "INSIDE_ARRAY_AFTER_COMMA":
3380:      case "INSIDE_ARRAY_AFTER_VALUE": {
3381:        result += "]";
3382:        break;
3383:      }
3384:      case "INSIDE_LITERAL": {
3385:        const partialLiteral = input.substring(literalStart, input.length);
3386:        if ("true".startsWith(partialLiteral)) {
3387:          result += "true".slice(partialLiteral.length);
3388:        } else if ("false".startsWith(partialLiteral)) {
3389:          result += "false".slice(partialLiteral.length);
3390:        } else if ("null".startsWith(partialLiteral)) {
3391:          result += "null".slice(partialLiteral.length);
3392:        }
3393:      }
3394:    }
3395:  }
3396:  return result;

3951:async function toResponseMessages({
3952:  content: inputContent,

3962:      continue;

3965:      continue;

3973:        });

3975:      case "reasoning":
3976:        content.push({
3977:          type: "reasoning",
3978:          text: part.text,
3979:          providerOptions: part.providerMetadata
3980:        });
3981:        break;
3982:      case "file":
3983:        content.push({
3984:          type: "file",
3985:          data: part.file.base64,
3986:          mediaType: part.file.mediaType,
3987:          providerOptions: part.providerMetadata
3988:        });
3989:        break;
3990:      case "tool-call":
3991:        content.push({
3992:          type: "tool-call",

3994:          toolName: part.toolName,
3995:          input: part.invalid && typeof part.input !== "object" ? {} : part.input,
3996:          providerExecuted: part.providerExecuted,
3997:          providerOptions: part.providerMetadata
3998:        });
3999:        break;
4000:      case "tool-result": {
4001:        const output = await createToolModelOutput({
4002:          toolCallId: part.toolCallId,
4003:          input: part.input,

4007:        });
4008:        content.push({
4009:          type: "tool-result",
4010:          toolCallId: part.toolCallId,
4011:          toolName: part.toolName,
4012:          output,
4013:          providerOptions: part.providerMetadata
4014:        });
4015:        break;
4016:      }
4017:      case "tool-error": {
4018:        const output = await createToolModelOutput({
4019:          toolCallId: part.toolCallId,
4020:          input: part.input,
4021:          tool: tools == null ? void 0 : tools[part.toolName],
4022:          output: part.error,
4023:          errorMode: "json"
4024:        });
4025:        content.push({
4026:          type: "tool-result",
4027:          toolCallId: part.toolCallId,
4028:          toolName: part.toolName,
4029:          output,
4030:          providerOptions: part.providerMetadata
4031:        });
4032:        break;
4033:      }
4034:      case "tool-approval-request":
4035:        content.push({
4036:          type: "tool-approval-request",

4045:      role: "assistant",

4047:    });

4051:    if (!(part.type === "tool-result" || part.type === "tool-error") || part.providerExecuted) {

4055:      toolCallId: part.toolCallId,

4057:      tool: tools == null ? void 0 : tools[part.toolName],

4078:// src/util/merge-abort-signals.ts
4079:function mergeAbortSignals(...signals) {
4080:  const validSignals = signals.filter(
4081:    (signal) => signal != null
4082:  );
4083:  if (validSignals.length === 0) {
4084:    return void 0;
4085:  }
4086:  if (validSignals.length === 1) {
4087:    return validSignals[0];
4088:  }
4089:  const controller = new AbortController();
4090:  for (const signal of validSignals) {
4091:    if (signal.aborted) {
4092:      controller.abort(signal.reason);
4093:      return controller.signal;
4094:    }
4095:    signal.addEventListener(
4096:      "abort",
4097:      () => {
4098:        controller.abort(signal.reason);
4099:      },
4100:      { once: true }
4101:    );
4102:  }
4103:  return controller.signal;
4104:}

4868:function asToolCalls(content) {
4869:  const parts = content.filter(
4870:    (part) => part.type === "tool-call"
4871:  );
4872:  if (parts.length === 0) {
4873:    return void 0;
4874:  }
4875:  return parts.map((toolCall) => ({
4876:    toolCallId: toolCall.toolCallId,
4877:    toolName: toolCall.toolName,
4878:    input: toolCall.input
4879:  }));
4880:}
4881:function asContent({
4882:  content,
4883:  toolCalls,
4884:  toolOutputs,
4885:  toolApprovalRequests,
4886:  tools
4887:}) {
4888:  const contentParts = [];
4889:  for (const part of content) {
4890:    switch (part.type) {
4891:      case "text":
4892:      case "reasoning":
4893:      case "source":
4894:        contentParts.push(part);
4895:        break;
4896:      case "file": {
4897:        contentParts.push({
4898:          type: "file",
4899:          file: new DefaultGeneratedFile(part),
4900:          ...part.providerMetadata != null ? { providerMetadata: part.providerMetadata } : {}
4901:        });
4902:        break;
4903:      }
4904:      case "tool-call": {
4905:        contentParts.push(
4906:          toolCalls.find((toolCall) => toolCall.toolCallId === part.toolCallId)
4907:        );
4908:        break;
4909:      }
4910:      case "tool-result": {
4911:        const toolCall = toolCalls.find(
4912:          (toolCall2) => toolCall2.toolCallId === part.toolCallId
4913:        );
4914:        if (toolCall == null) {
4915:          const tool2 = tools == null ? void 0 : tools[part.toolName];
4916:          const supportsDeferredResults = (tool2 == null ? void 0 : tool2.type) === "provider" && tool2.supportsDeferredResults;
4917:          if (!supportsDeferredResults) {
4918:            throw new Error(`Tool call ${part.toolCallId} not found.`);
4919:          }
4920:          if (part.isError) {
4921:            contentParts.push({
4922:              type: "tool-error",
4923:              toolCallId: part.toolCallId,
4924:              toolName: part.toolName,
4925:              input: void 0,
4926:              error: part.result,
4927:              providerExecuted: true,
4928:              dynamic: part.dynamic,
4929:              ...part.providerMetadata != null ? { providerMetadata: part.providerMetadata } : {}
4930:            });
4931:          } else {
4932:            contentParts.push({
4933:              type: "tool-result",
4934:              toolCallId: part.toolCallId,
4935:              toolName: part.toolName,
4936:              input: void 0,
4937:              output: part.result,
4938:              providerExecuted: true,
4939:              dynamic: part.dynamic,
4940:              ...part.providerMetadata != null ? { providerMetadata: part.providerMetadata } : {}
4941:            });
4942:          }
4943:          break;
4944:        }
4945:        if (part.isError) {
4946:          contentParts.push({
4947:            type: "tool-error",
4948:            toolCallId: part.toolCallId,
4949:            toolName: part.toolName,
4950:            input: toolCall.input,
4951:            error: part.result,
4952:            providerExecuted: true,
4953:            dynamic: toolCall.dynamic,
4954:            ...part.providerMetadata != null ? { providerMetadata: part.providerMetadata } : {}
4955:          });
4956:        } else {
4957:          contentParts.push({
4958:            type: "tool-result",
4959:            toolCallId: part.toolCallId,
4960:            toolName: part.toolName,
4961:            input: toolCall.input,
4962:            output: part.result,
4963:            providerExecuted: true,
4964:            dynamic: toolCall.dynamic,
4965:            ...part.providerMetadata != null ? { providerMetadata: part.providerMetadata } : {}
4966:          });
4967:        }
4968:        break;
4969:      }
4970:      case "tool-approval-request": {
4971:        const toolCall = toolCalls.find(
4972:          (toolCall2) => toolCall2.toolCallId === part.toolCallId
4973:        );
4974:        if (toolCall == null) {
4975:          throw new ToolCallNotFoundForApprovalError({
4976:            toolCallId: part.toolCallId,
4977:            approvalId: part.approvalId
4978:          });
4979:        }
4980:        contentParts.push({
4981:          type: "tool-approval-request",
4982:          approvalId: part.approvalId,
4983:          toolCall
4984:        });
4985:        break;
4986:      }
4987:    }
4988:  }
4989:  return [...contentParts, ...toolOutputs, ...toolApprovalRequests];
4990:}

5023:// src/util/write-to-server-response.ts
5024:function writeToServerResponse({
5025:  response,
5026:  status,
5027:  statusText,
5028:  headers,
5029:  stream
5030:}) {
5031:  const statusCode = status != null ? status : 200;
5032:  if (statusText !== void 0) {
5033:    response.writeHead(statusCode, statusText, headers);
5034:  } else {
5035:    response.writeHead(statusCode, headers);
5036:  }
5037:  const reader = stream.getReader();
5038:  const read = async () => {
5039:    try {
5040:      while (true) {
5041:        const { done, value } = await reader.read();
5042:        if (done)
5043:          break;
5044:        const canContinue = response.write(value);
5045:        if (!canContinue) {
5046:          await new Promise((resolve3) => {
5047:            response.once("drain", resolve3);
5048:          });
5049:        }
5050:      }
5051:    } catch (error) {
5052:      throw error;
5053:    } finally {
5054:      response.end();
5055:    }
5056:  };
5057:  read();
5058:}

6019:function createAsyncIterableStream(source) {
6020:  const stream = source.pipeThrough(new TransformStream());
6021:  stream[Symbol.asyncIterator] = function() {
6022:    const reader = this.getReader();
6023:    let finished = false;

6026:      if (finished)
6027:        return;
6028:      finished = true;
6029:      try {
6030:        if (cancelStream) {
6031:          await ((_a21 = reader.cancel) == null ? void 0 : _a21.call(reader));
6032:        }

6034:        try {
6035:          reader.releaseLock();
6036:        } catch (e) {
6037:        }
6038:      }
6039:    }

6041:      /**
6042:       * Reads the next chunk from the stream.
6043:       * @returns A promise resolving to the next IteratorResult.
6044:       */
6045:      async next() {
6046:        if (finished) {
6047:          return { done: true, value: void 0 };
6048:        }

6052:          return { done: true, value: void 0 };
6053:        }
6054:        return { done: false, value };
6055:      },
6056:      /**
6057:       * May be called on early exit (e.g., break from for-await) or after completion.
6058:       * Ensures the stream is cancelled and resources are released.
6059:       * @returns A promise resolving to a completed IteratorResult.
6060:       */
6061:      async return() {
6062:        await cleanup(true);
6063:        return { done: true, value: void 0 };
6064:      },
6065:      /**
6066:       * Called on early exit with error.
6067:       * Ensures the stream is cancelled and resources are released, then rethrows the error.
6068:       * @param err The error to throw.
6069:       * @returns A promise that rejects with the provided error.
6070:       */
6071:      async throw(err) {
6072:        await cleanup(true);
6073:        throw err;
6074:      }

6094:  } finally {

6114:// src/util/create-stitchable-stream.ts
6115:function createStitchableStream() {
6116:  let innerStreamReaders = [];
6117:  let controller = null;
6118:  let isClosed = false;
6119:  let waitForNewStream = createResolvablePromise();
6120:  const terminate = () => {
6121:    isClosed = true;
6122:    waitForNewStream.resolve();
6123:    innerStreamReaders.forEach((reader) => reader.cancel());
6124:    innerStreamReaders = [];
6125:    controller == null ? void 0 : controller.close();
6126:  };
6127:  const processPull = async () => {
6128:    if (isClosed && innerStreamReaders.length === 0) {
6129:      controller == null ? void 0 : controller.close();
6130:      return;
6131:    }
6132:    if (innerStreamReaders.length === 0) {
6133:      waitForNewStream = createResolvablePromise();
6134:      await waitForNewStream.promise;
6135:      return processPull();
6136:    }
6137:    try {
6138:      const { value, done } = await innerStreamReaders[0].read();
6139:      if (done) {
6140:        innerStreamReaders.shift();
6141:        if (innerStreamReaders.length === 0 && isClosed) {
6142:          controller == null ? void 0 : controller.close();
6143:        } else {
6144:          await processPull();
6145:        }
6146:      } else {
6147:        controller == null ? void 0 : controller.enqueue(value);
6148:      }
6149:    } catch (error) {
6150:      controller == null ? void 0 : controller.error(error);
6151:      innerStreamReaders.shift();
6152:      terminate();
6153:    }
6154:  };
6155:  return {
6156:    stream: new ReadableStream({
6157:      start(controllerParam) {
6158:        controller = controllerParam;
6159:      },
6160:      pull: processPull,
6161:      async cancel() {
6162:        for (const reader of innerStreamReaders) {
6163:          await reader.cancel();
6164:        }
6165:        innerStreamReaders = [];
6166:        isClosed = true;
6167:      }
6168:    }),
6169:    addStream: (innerStream) => {
6170:      if (isClosed) {
6171:        throw new Error("Cannot add inner stream: outer stream is closed");
6172:      }
6173:      innerStreamReaders.push(innerStream.getReader());
6174:      waitForNewStream.resolve();
6175:    },
6176:    /**
6177:     * Gracefully close the outer stream. This will let the inner streams
6178:     * finish processing and then close the outer stream.
6179:     */
6180:    close: () => {
6181:      isClosed = true;
6182:      waitForNewStream.resolve();
6183:      if (innerStreamReaders.length === 0) {
6184:        controller == null ? void 0 : controller.close();
6185:      }
6186:    },
6187:    /**
6188:     * Immediately close the outer stream. This will cancel all inner streams
6189:     * and close the outer stream.
6190:     */
6191:    terminate
6192:  };
6193:}

8886:async function safeValidateUIMessages({
8887:  messages,
8888:  metadataSchema,
8889:  dataSchemas,
8890:  tools
8891:}) {
8892:  try {
8893:    if (messages == null) {
8894:      return {
8895:        success: false,
8896:        error: new InvalidArgumentError({
8897:          parameter: "messages",
8898:          value: messages,
8899:          message: "messages parameter must be provided"
8900:        })
8901:      };
8902:    }
8903:    const validatedMessages = await (0, import_provider_utils22.validateTypes)({
8904:      value: messages,
8905:      schema: uiMessagesSchema
8906:    });
8907:    if (metadataSchema) {
8908:      for (const [msgIdx, message] of validatedMessages.entries()) {
8909:        await (0, import_provider_utils22.validateTypes)({
8910:          value: message.metadata,
8911:          schema: metadataSchema,
8912:          context: {
8913:            field: `messages[${msgIdx}].metadata`,
8914:            entityId: message.id
8915:          }
8916:        });
8917:      }
8918:    }
8919:    if (dataSchemas || tools) {
8920:      for (const [msgIdx, message] of validatedMessages.entries()) {
8921:        for (const [partIdx, part] of message.parts.entries()) {
8922:          if (dataSchemas && part.type.startsWith("data-")) {
8923:            const dataPart = part;
8924:            const dataName = dataPart.type.slice(5);
8925:            const dataSchema = dataSchemas[dataName];
8926:            if (!dataSchema) {
8927:              return {
8928:                success: false,
8929:                error: new import_provider29.TypeValidationError({
8930:                  value: dataPart.data,
8931:                  cause: `No data schema found for data part ${dataName}`,
8932:                  context: {
8933:                    field: `messages[${msgIdx}].parts[${partIdx}].data`,
8934:                    entityName: dataName,
8935:                    entityId: dataPart.id
8936:                  }
8937:                })
8938:              };
8939:            }
8940:            await (0, import_provider_utils22.validateTypes)({
8941:              value: dataPart.data,
8942:              schema: dataSchema,
8943:              context: {
8944:                field: `messages[${msgIdx}].parts[${partIdx}].data`,
8945:                entityName: dataName,
8946:                entityId: dataPart.id
8947:              }
8948:            });
8949:          }
8950:          if (tools && part.type.startsWith("tool-")) {
8951:            const toolPart = part;
8952:            const toolName = toolPart.type.slice(5);
8953:            const tool2 = tools[toolName];
8954:            if (!tool2) {
8955:              return {
8956:                success: false,
8957:                error: new import_provider29.TypeValidationError({
8958:                  value: toolPart.input,
8959:                  cause: `No tool schema found for tool part ${toolName}`,
8960:                  context: {
8961:                    field: `messages[${msgIdx}].parts[${partIdx}].input`,
8962:                    entityName: toolName,
8963:                    entityId: toolPart.toolCallId
8964:                  }
8965:                })
8966:              };
8967:            }
8968:            if (toolPart.state === "input-available" || toolPart.state === "output-available" || toolPart.state === "output-error" && toolPart.input !== void 0) {
8969:              await (0, import_provider_utils22.validateTypes)({
8970:                value: toolPart.input,
8971:                schema: tool2.inputSchema,
8972:                context: {
8973:                  field: `messages[${msgIdx}].parts[${partIdx}].input`,
8974:                  entityName: toolName,
8975:                  entityId: toolPart.toolCallId
8976:                }
8977:              });
8978:            }
8979:            if (toolPart.state === "output-available" && tool2.outputSchema) {
8980:              await (0, import_provider_utils22.validateTypes)({
8981:                value: toolPart.output,
8982:                schema: tool2.outputSchema,
8983:                context: {
8984:                  field: `messages[${msgIdx}].parts[${partIdx}].output`,
8985:                  entityName: toolName,
8986:                  entityId: toolPart.toolCallId
8987:                }
8988:              });
8989:            }
8990:          }
8991:        }
8992:      }
8993:    }
8994:    return {
8995:      success: true,
8996:      data: validatedMessages
8997:    };
8998:  } catch (error) {
8999:    const err = error;
9000:    return {
9001:      success: false,
9002:      error: err
9003:    };
9004:  }
9005:}
9006:async function validateUIMessages({
9007:  messages,
9008:  metadataSchema,
9009:  dataSchemas,
9010:  tools
9011:}) {
9012:  const response = await safeValidateUIMessages({
9013:    messages,
9014:    metadataSchema,
9015:    dataSchemas,
9016:    tools
9017:  });
9018:  if (!response.success)
9019:    throw response.error;
9020:  return response.data;
9021:}

10377:// src/util/cosine-similarity.ts
10378:function cosineSimilarity(vector1, vector2) {
10379:  if (vector1.length !== vector2.length) {
10380:    throw new InvalidArgumentError({
10381:      parameter: "vector1,vector2",
10382:      value: { vector1Length: vector1.length, vector2Length: vector2.length },
10383:      message: `Vectors must have the same length`
10384:    });
10385:  }
10386:  const n = vector1.length;
10387:  if (n === 0) {
10388:    return 0;
10389:  }
10390:  let magnitudeSquared1 = 0;
10391:  let magnitudeSquared2 = 0;
10392:  let dotProduct = 0;
10393:  for (let i = 0; i < n; i++) {
10394:    const value1 = vector1[i];
10395:    const value2 = vector2[i];
10396:    magnitudeSquared1 += value1 * value1;
10397:    magnitudeSquared2 += value2 * value2;
10398:    dotProduct += value1 * value2;
10399:  }
10400:  return magnitudeSquared1 === 0 || magnitudeSquared2 === 0 ? 0 : dotProduct / (Math.sqrt(magnitudeSquared1) * Math.sqrt(magnitudeSquared2));
10401:}

10409:function getTextFromDataUrl(dataUrl) {
10410:  const [header, base64Content] = dataUrl.split(",");
10411:  const mediaType = header.split(";")[0].split(":")[1];
10412:  if (mediaType == null || base64Content == null) {
10413:    throw new Error("Invalid data URL format");
10414:  }
10415:  try {
10416:    return window.atob(base64Content);
10417:  } catch (error) {
10418:    throw new Error(`Error decoding data URL`);
10419:  }

10422:// src/util/is-deep-equal-data.ts
10423:function isDeepEqualData(obj1, obj2) {
10424:  if (obj1 === obj2)
10425:    return true;
10426:  if (obj1 == null || obj2 == null)
10427:    return false;
10428:  if (typeof obj1 !== "object" && typeof obj2 !== "object")
10429:    return obj1 === obj2;
10430:  if (obj1.constructor !== obj2.constructor)
10431:    return false;
10432:  if (obj1 instanceof Date && obj2 instanceof Date) {
10433:    return obj1.getTime() === obj2.getTime();
10434:  }
10435:  if (Array.isArray(obj1)) {
10436:    if (obj1.length !== obj2.length)
10437:      return false;
10438:    for (let i = 0; i < obj1.length; i++) {
10439:      if (!isDeepEqualData(obj1[i], obj2[i]))
10440:        return false;
10441:    }
10442:    return true;
10443:  }
10444:  const keys1 = Object.keys(obj1);
10445:  const keys2 = Object.keys(obj2);
10446:  if (keys1.length !== keys2.length)
10447:    return false;
10448:  for (const key of keys1) {
10449:    if (!keys2.includes(key))
10450:      return false;
10451:    if (!isDeepEqualData(obj1[key], obj2[key]))
10452:      return false;
10453:  }
10454:  return true;
10455:}

10458:var SerialJobExecutor = class {
10459:  constructor() {
10460:    this.queue = [];
10461:    this.isProcessing = false;
10462:  }
10463:  async processQueue() {
10464:    if (this.isProcessing) {
10465:      return;
10466:    }
10467:    this.isProcessing = true;
10468:    while (this.queue.length > 0) {
10469:      await this.queue[0]();
10470:      this.queue.shift();
10471:    }
10472:    this.isProcessing = false;
10473:  }
10474:  async run(job) {
10475:    return new Promise((resolve3, reject) => {
10476:      this.queue.push(async () => {
10477:        try {
10478:          await job();
10479:          resolve3();
10480:        } catch (error) {
10481:          reject(error);
10482:        }
10483:      });
10484:      void this.processQueue();
10485:    });
10486:  }
10487:};

11136:function pruneMessages({
11137:  messages,
11138:  reasoning = "none",
11139:  toolCalls = [],
11140:  emptyMessages = "remove"
11141:}) {
11142:  if (reasoning === "all" || reasoning === "before-last-message") {
11143:    messages = messages.map((message, messageIndex) => {
11144:      if (message.role !== "assistant" || typeof message.content === "string" || reasoning === "before-last-message" && messageIndex === messages.length - 1) {
11145:        return message;
11146:      }
11147:      return {
11148:        ...message,
11149:        content: message.content.filter((part) => part.type !== "reasoning")
11150:      };
11151:    });
11152:  }
11153:  if (toolCalls === "none") {
11154:    toolCalls = [];
11155:  } else if (toolCalls === "all") {
11156:    toolCalls = [{ type: "all" }];
11157:  } else if (toolCalls === "before-last-message") {
11158:    toolCalls = [{ type: "before-last-message" }];
11159:  } else if (typeof toolCalls === "string") {
11160:    toolCalls = [{ type: toolCalls }];
11161:  }
11162:  for (const toolCall of toolCalls) {
11163:    const keepLastMessagesCount = toolCall.type === "all" ? void 0 : toolCall.type === "before-last-message" ? 1 : Number(
11164:      toolCall.type.slice("before-last-".length).slice(0, -"-messages".length)
11165:    );
11166:    const keptToolCallIds = /* @__PURE__ */ new Set();
11167:    const keptApprovalIds = /* @__PURE__ */ new Set();
11168:    if (keepLastMessagesCount != null) {
11169:      for (const message of messages.slice(-keepLastMessagesCount)) {
11170:        if ((message.role === "assistant" || message.role === "tool") && typeof message.content !== "string") {
11171:          for (const part of message.content) {
11172:            if (part.type === "tool-call" || part.type === "tool-result") {
11173:              keptToolCallIds.add(part.toolCallId);
11174:            } else if (part.type === "tool-approval-request" || part.type === "tool-approval-response") {
11175:              keptApprovalIds.add(part.approvalId);
11176:            }
11177:          }
11178:        }
11179:      }
11180:    }
11181:    messages = messages.map((message, messageIndex) => {
11182:      if (message.role !== "assistant" && message.role !== "tool" || typeof message.content === "string" || keepLastMessagesCount && messageIndex >= messages.length - keepLastMessagesCount) {
11183:        return message;
11184:      }
11185:      const toolCallIdToToolName = {};
11186:      const approvalIdToToolName = {};
11187:      return {
11188:        ...message,
11189:        content: message.content.filter((part) => {
11190:          if (part.type !== "tool-call" && part.type !== "tool-result" && part.type !== "tool-approval-request" && part.type !== "tool-approval-response") {
11191:            return true;
11192:          }
11193:          if (part.type === "tool-call") {
11194:            toolCallIdToToolName[part.toolCallId] = part.toolName;
11195:          } else if (part.type === "tool-approval-request") {
11196:            approvalIdToToolName[part.approvalId] = toolCallIdToToolName[part.toolCallId];
11197:          }
11198:          if ((part.type === "tool-call" || part.type === "tool-result") && keptToolCallIds.has(part.toolCallId) || (part.type === "tool-approval-request" || part.type === "tool-approval-response") && keptApprovalIds.has(part.approvalId)) {
11199:            return true;
11200:          }
11201:          return toolCall.tools != null && !toolCall.tools.includes(
11202:            part.type === "tool-call" || part.type === "tool-result" ? part.toolName : approvalIdToToolName[part.approvalId]
11203:          );
11204:        })
11205:      };
11206:    });
11207:  }
11208:  if (emptyMessages === "remove") {
11209:    messages = messages.filter((message) => message.content.length > 0);
11210:  }
11211:  return messages;

11214:// src/generate-text/smooth-stream.ts
11215:var import_provider_utils32 = require("@ai-sdk/provider-utils");
11216:var import_provider32 = require("@ai-sdk/provider");
11217:var CHUNKING_REGEXPS = {
11218:  word: /\S+\s+/m,
11219:  line: /\n+/m
11220:};
11221:function smoothStream({
11222:  delayInMs = 10,
11223:  chunking = "word",
11224:  _internal: { delay: delay2 = import_provider_utils32.delay } = {}
11225:} = {}) {
11226:  let detectChunk;
11227:  if (chunking != null && typeof chunking === "object" && "segment" in chunking && typeof chunking.segment === "function") {
11228:    const segmenter = chunking;
11229:    detectChunk = (buffer) => {
11230:      if (buffer.length === 0)
11231:        return null;
11232:      const iterator = segmenter.segment(buffer)[Symbol.iterator]();
11233:      const first = iterator.next().value;
11234:      return (first == null ? void 0 : first.segment) || null;
11235:    };
11236:  } else if (typeof chunking === "function") {
11237:    detectChunk = (buffer) => {
11238:      const match = chunking(buffer);
11239:      if (match == null) {
11240:        return null;
11241:      }
11242:      if (!match.length) {
11243:        throw new Error(`Chunking function must return a non-empty string.`);
11244:      }
11245:      if (!buffer.startsWith(match)) {
11246:        throw new Error(
11247:          `Chunking function must return a match that is a prefix of the buffer. Received: "${match}" expected to start with "${buffer}"`
11248:        );
11249:      }
11250:      return match;
11251:    };
11252:  } else {
11253:    const chunkingRegex = typeof chunking === "string" ? CHUNKING_REGEXPS[chunking] : chunking instanceof RegExp ? chunking : void 0;
11254:    if (chunkingRegex == null) {
11255:      throw new import_provider32.InvalidArgumentError({
11256:        argument: "chunking",
11257:        message: `Chunking must be "word", "line", a RegExp, an Intl.Segmenter, or a ChunkDetector function. Received: ${chunking}`
11258:      });
11259:    }
11260:    detectChunk = (buffer) => {
11261:      const match = chunkingRegex.exec(buffer);
11262:      if (!match) {
11263:        return null;
11264:      }
11265:      return buffer.slice(0, match.index) + (match == null ? void 0 : match[0]);
11266:    };
11267:  }
11268:  return () => {
11269:    let buffer = "";
11270:    let id = "";
11271:    let type = void 0;
11272:    let providerMetadata = void 0;
11273:    function flushBuffer(controller) {
11274:      if (buffer.length > 0 && type !== void 0) {
11275:        controller.enqueue({
11276:          type,
11277:          text: buffer,
11278:          id,
11279:          ...providerMetadata != null ? { providerMetadata } : {}
11280:        });
11281:        buffer = "";
11282:        providerMetadata = void 0;
11283:      }
11284:    }
11285:    return new TransformStream({
11286:      async transform(chunk, controller) {
11287:        if (chunk.type !== "text-delta" && chunk.type !== "reasoning-delta") {
11288:          flushBuffer(controller);
11289:          controller.enqueue(chunk);
11290:          return;
11291:        }
11292:        if ((chunk.type !== type || chunk.id !== id) && buffer.length > 0) {
11293:          flushBuffer(controller);
11294:        }
11295:        buffer += chunk.text;
11296:        id = chunk.id;
11297:        type = chunk.type;
11298:        if (chunk.providerMetadata != null) {
11299:          providerMetadata = chunk.providerMetadata;
11300:        }
11301:        let match;
11302:        while ((match = detectChunk(buffer)) != null) {
11303:          controller.enqueue({ type, text: match, id });
11304:          buffer = buffer.slice(match.length);
11305:          await delay2(delayInMs);
11306:        }
11307:      }
11308:    });
11309:  };
11310:}

11622:                  }

11671:// src/util/get-potential-start-index.ts
11672:function getPotentialStartIndex(text2, searchedText) {
11673:  if (searchedText.length === 0) {
11674:    return null;
11675:  }
11676:  const directIndex = text2.indexOf(searchedText);
11677:  if (directIndex !== -1) {
11678:    return directIndex;
11679:  }
11680:  for (let i = text2.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
11681:    const suffix = text2.substring(i);
11682:    if (searchedText.startsWith(suffix)) {
11683:      return i;
11684:    }
11685:  }
11686:  return null;

11689:// src/middleware/extract-reasoning-middleware.ts
11690:function extractReasoningMiddleware({
11691:  tagName,
11692:  separator = "\n",
11693:  startWithReasoning = false
11694:}) {
11695:  const openingTag = `<${tagName}>`;
11696:  const closingTag = `</${tagName}>`;
11697:  return {
11698:    specificationVersion: "v3",
11699:    wrapGenerate: async ({ doGenerate }) => {
11700:      const { content, ...rest } = await doGenerate();
11701:      const transformedContent = [];
11702:      for (const part of content) {
11703:        if (part.type !== "text") {
11704:          transformedContent.push(part);
11705:          continue;
11706:        }
11707:        const text2 = startWithReasoning ? openingTag + part.text : part.text;
11708:        const regexp = new RegExp(`${openingTag}(.*?)${closingTag}`, "gs");
11709:        const matches = Array.from(text2.matchAll(regexp));
11710:        if (!matches.length) {
11711:          transformedContent.push(part);
11712:          continue;
11713:        }
11714:        const reasoningText = matches.map((match) => match[1]).join(separator);
11715:        let textWithoutReasoning = text2;
11716:        for (let i = matches.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
11717:          const match = matches[i];
11718:          const beforeMatch = textWithoutReasoning.slice(0, match.index);
11719:          const afterMatch = textWithoutReasoning.slice(
11720:            match.index + match[0].length
11721:          );
11722:          textWithoutReasoning = beforeMatch + (beforeMatch.length > 0 && afterMatch.length > 0 ? separator : "") + afterMatch;
11723:        }
11724:        transformedContent.push({
11725:          type: "reasoning",
11726:          text: reasoningText
11727:        });
11728:        transformedContent.push({
11729:          type: "text",
11730:          text: textWithoutReasoning
11731:        });
11732:      }
11733:      return { content: transformedContent, ...rest };
11734:    },
11735:    wrapStream: async ({ doStream }) => {
11736:      const { stream, ...rest } = await doStream();
11737:      const reasoningExtractions = {};
11738:      let delayedTextStart;
11739:      return {
11740:        stream: stream.pipeThrough(
11741:          new TransformStream({
11742:            transform: (chunk, controller) => {
11743:              if (chunk.type === "text-start") {
11744:                delayedTextStart = chunk;
11745:                return;
11746:              }
11747:              if (chunk.type === "text-end" && delayedTextStart) {
11748:                controller.enqueue(delayedTextStart);
11749:                delayedTextStart = void 0;
11750:              }
11751:              if (chunk.type !== "text-delta") {
11752:                controller.enqueue(chunk);
11753:                return;
11754:              }
11755:              if (reasoningExtractions[chunk.id] == null) {
11756:                reasoningExtractions[chunk.id] = {
11757:                  isFirstReasoning: true,
11758:                  isFirstText: true,
11759:                  afterSwitch: false,
11760:                  isReasoning: startWithReasoning,
11761:                  buffer: "",
11762:                  idCounter: 0,
11763:                  textId: chunk.id
11764:                };
11765:              }
11766:              const activeExtraction = reasoningExtractions[chunk.id];
11767:              activeExtraction.buffer += chunk.delta;
11768:              function publish(text2) {
11769:                if (text2.length > 0) {
11770:                  const prefix = activeExtraction.afterSwitch && (activeExtraction.isReasoning ? !activeExtraction.isFirstReasoning : !activeExtraction.isFirstText) ? separator : "";
11771:                  if (activeExtraction.isReasoning && (activeExtraction.afterSwitch || activeExtraction.isFirstReasoning)) {
11772:                    controller.enqueue({
11773:                      type: "reasoning-start",
11774:                      id: `reasoning-${activeExtraction.idCounter}`
11775:                    });
11776:                  }
11777:                  if (activeExtraction.isReasoning) {
11778:                    controller.enqueue({
11779:                      type: "reasoning-delta",
11780:                      delta: prefix + text2,
11781:                      id: `reasoning-${activeExtraction.idCounter}`
11782:                    });
11783:                  } else {
11784:                    if (delayedTextStart) {
11785:                      controller.enqueue(delayedTextStart);
11786:                      delayedTextStart = void 0;
11787:                    }
11788:                    controller.enqueue({
11789:                      type: "text-delta",
11790:                      delta: prefix + text2,
11791:                      id: activeExtraction.textId
11792:                    });
11793:                  }
11794:                  activeExtraction.afterSwitch = false;
11795:                  if (activeExtraction.isReasoning) {
11796:                    activeExtraction.isFirstReasoning = false;
11797:                  } else {
11798:                    activeExtraction.isFirstText = false;
11799:                  }
11800:                }
11801:              }
11802:              do {
11803:                const nextTag = activeExtraction.isReasoning ? closingTag : openingTag;
11804:                const startIndex = getPotentialStartIndex(
11805:                  activeExtraction.buffer,
11806:                  nextTag
11807:                );
11808:                if (startIndex == null) {
11809:                  publish(activeExtraction.buffer);
11810:                  activeExtraction.buffer = "";
11811:                  break;
11812:                }
11813:                publish(activeExtraction.buffer.slice(0, startIndex));
11814:                const foundFullMatch = startIndex + nextTag.length <= activeExtraction.buffer.length;
11815:                if (foundFullMatch) {
11816:                  activeExtraction.buffer = activeExtraction.buffer.slice(
11817:                    startIndex + nextTag.length
11818:                  );
11819:                  if (activeExtraction.isReasoning) {
11820:                    if (activeExtraction.isFirstReasoning) {
11821:                      controller.enqueue({
11822:                        type: "reasoning-start",
11823:                        id: `reasoning-${activeExtraction.idCounter}`
11824:                      });
11825:                    }
11826:                    controller.enqueue({
11827:                      type: "reasoning-end",
11828:                      id: `reasoning-${activeExtraction.idCounter++}`
11829:                    });
11830:                  }
11831:                  activeExtraction.isReasoning = !activeExtraction.isReasoning;
11832:                  activeExtraction.afterSwitch = true;
11833:                } else {
11834:                  activeExtraction.buffer = activeExtraction.buffer.slice(startIndex);
11835:                  break;
11836:                }

11838:            }
11839:          })
11840:        ),
11841:        ...rest
11842:      };

12660:        (0, import_provider_utils35.getRuntimeEnvironmentUserAgent)()
12661:      ),
12662:      signal: abortController.signal
12663:    }).catch((err) => {
12664:      throw err;
12665:    });
12666:    if (!response.ok) {
12667:      throw new Error(
12668:        (_a21 = await response.text()) != null ? _a21 : "Failed to fetch the chat response."
12669:      );
12670:    }
12671:    if (!response.body) {
12672:      throw new Error("The response body is empty.");
12673:    }
12674:    let result = "";
12675:    switch (streamProtocol) {
12676:      case "text": {
12677:        await processTextStream({
12678:          stream: response.body,
12679:          onTextPart: (chunk) => {
12680:            result += chunk;
12681:            setCompletion(result);
12682:          }
12683:        });
12684:        break;
12685:      }
12686:      case "data": {
12687:        await consumeStream({
12688:          stream: (0, import_provider_utils35.parseJsonEventStream)({
12689:            stream: response.body,
12690:            schema: uiMessageChunkSchema
12691:          }).pipeThrough(
12692:            new TransformStream({
12693:              async transform(part) {
12694:                if (!part.success) {
12695:                  throw part.error;
12696:                }
12697:                const streamPart = part.value;
12698:                if (streamPart.type === "text-delta") {
12699:                  result += streamPart.delta;
12700:                  setCompletion(result);
12701:                } else if (streamPart.type === "error") {
12702:                  throw new Error(streamPart.errorText);
12703:                }
12704:              }
12705:            })
12706:          ),
12707:          onError: (error) => {
12708:            throw error;
12709:          }
12710:        });
12711:        break;
12712:      }
12713:      default: {
12714:        const exhaustiveCheck = streamProtocol;
12715:        throw new Error(`Unknown stream protocol: ${exhaustiveCheck}`);
12716:      }
12717:    }
12718:    if (onFinish) {
12719:      onFinish(prompt, result);
12720:    }
12721:    setAbortController(null);
12722:    return result;
12723:  } catch (err) {
12724:    if (err.name === "AbortError") {
12725:      setAbortController(null);
12726:      return null;
12727:    }
12728:    if (err instanceof Error) {
12729:      if (onError) {
12730:        onError(err);
12731:      }
12732:    }
12733:    setError(err);
12734:  } finally {
12735:    setLoading(false);
12736:  }
12737:}

13184:        }

13187:      }

13192:    let isDisconnect = false;
13193:    let isError = false;
13194:    try {
13195:      const activeResponse = {
13196:        state: createStreamingUIMessageState({

13198:          messageId: this.generateId()
13199:        }),

13203:        isAbort = true;

13222:        // serialize the job execution to avoid race conditions:

13276:          message: this.activeResponse.state.message,
13277:          messages: this.state.messages,
13278:          isAbort,
13279:          isDisconnect,
13280:          isError,
13281:          finishReason: (_a21 = this.activeResponse) == null ? void 0 : _a21.state.finishReason
13282:        });
13283:      } catch (err) {
13284:        console.error(err);
13285:      }
13286:      this.activeResponse = void 0;
13287:    }
13288:    if (!isError && await this.shouldSendAutomatically()) {
13289:      await this.makeRequest({
13290:        trigger: "submit-message",
13291:        messageId: (_c = this.lastMessage) == null ? void 0 : _c.id,
13292:        metadata,
13293:        headers,
13294:        body

13300:// src/ui/direct-chat-transport.ts
13301:var DirectChatTransport = class {
13302:  constructor({
13303:    agent,
13304:    options,
13305:    ...uiMessageStreamOptions
13306:  }) {
13307:    this.agent = agent;
13308:    this.agentOptions = options;
13309:    this.uiMessageStreamOptions = uiMessageStreamOptions;
13310:  }
13311:  async sendMessages({
13312:    messages,
13313:    abortSignal
13314:  }) {
13315:    const validatedMessages = await validateUIMessages({
13316:      messages,
13317:      tools: this.agent.tools
13318:    });
13319:    const modelMessages = await convertToModelMessages(validatedMessages, {
13320:      tools: this.agent.tools
13321:    });
13322:    const result = await this.agent.stream({
13323:      prompt: modelMessages,
13324:      abortSignal,
13325:      ...this.agentOptions !== void 0 ? { options: this.agentOptions } : {}
13326:    });
13327:    return result.toUIMessageStream(this.uiMessageStreamOptions);
13328:  }
13329:  /**
13330:   * Direct transport does not support reconnection since there is no
13331:   * persistent server-side stream to reconnect to.
13332:   *
13333:   * @returns Always returns `null`
13334:   */
13335:  async reconnectToStream(_options) {
13336:    return null;
13337:  }

13340:// src/ui/last-assistant-message-is-complete-with-approval-responses.ts
13341:function lastAssistantMessageIsCompleteWithApprovalResponses({
13342:  messages
13343:}) {
13344:  const message = messages[messages.length - 1];
13345:  if (!message) {
13346:    return false;
13347:  }
13348:  if (message.role !== "assistant") {
13349:    return false;
13350:  }
13351:  const lastStepStartIndex = message.parts.reduce((lastIndex, part, index) => {
13352:    return part.type === "step-start" ? index : lastIndex;
13353:  }, -1);
13354:  const lastStepToolInvocations = message.parts.slice(lastStepStartIndex + 1).filter(isToolUIPart);
13355:  return (
13356:    // has at least one tool approval response
13357:    lastStepToolInvocations.filter((part) => part.state === "approval-responded").length > 0 && // all tool approvals must have a response
13358:    lastStepToolInvocations.every(
13359:      (part) => part.state === "output-available" || part.state === "output-error" || part.state === "approval-responded"
13360:    )
13361:  );
13362:}
13364:// src/ui/last-assistant-message-is-complete-with-tool-calls.ts
13365:function lastAssistantMessageIsCompleteWithToolCalls({
13366:  messages
13367:}) {
13368:  const message = messages[messages.length - 1];
13369:  if (!message) {
13370:    return false;
13371:  }
13372:  if (message.role !== "assistant") {
13373:    return false;
13374:  }
13375:  const lastStepStartIndex = message.parts.reduce((lastIndex, part, index) => {
13376:    return part.type === "step-start" ? index : lastIndex;
13377:  }, -1);
13378:  const lastStepToolInvocations = message.parts.slice(lastStepStartIndex + 1).filter(isToolUIPart).filter((part) => !part.providerExecuted);
13379:  return lastStepToolInvocations.length > 0 && lastStepToolInvocations.every(
13380:    (part) => part.state === "output-available" || part.state === "output-error"
13381:  );
13382:}
13384:// src/ui/transform-text-to-ui-message-stream.ts
13385:function transformTextToUiMessageStream({
13386:  stream
13387:}) {
13388:  return stream.pipeThrough(
13389:    new TransformStream({
13390:      start(controller) {
13391:        controller.enqueue({ type: "start" });
13392:        controller.enqueue({ type: "start-step" });
13393:        controller.enqueue({ type: "text-start", id: "text-1" });
13394:      },
13395:      async transform(part, controller) {
13396:        controller.enqueue({ type: "text-delta", id: "text-1", delta: part });
13397:      },
13398:      async flush(controller) {
13399:        controller.enqueue({ type: "text-end", id: "text-1" });
13400:        controller.enqueue({ type: "finish-step" });
13401:        controller.enqueue({ type: "finish" });
13402:      }
13403:    })
13404:  );
13405:}
